[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Organization)

:   "*The Council will act as they deem necessary.*"
:   ―Mace Windu[[7]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-7)

The **Jedi High Council**, more commonly known as the **Jedi Council**, was a [body](/wiki/Jedi_Council "Jedi Council") of twelve [Jedi Masters](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") that governed the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). Headquartered in the [Jedi Grand Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), the High Council worked with the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") to maintain peace and justice in the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"). In addition, the High Council tracked the progress of the [Jedi training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") of [Padawans](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan"), deciding when the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") was right for an apprentice to undergo the [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials") in order to attain the rank of [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight"), and from there, the rank of Master. The High Council also enforced the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code") and traditionally selected its own members, including the [Master of the Order](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order") who functioned as the body's elected leader. During the late [Republic Era](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era"), legendary Jedi Masters, such as [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi"), and [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master") [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") comprised the High Council.

The High Council adopted a [leadership role](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") in the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") as a result of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), working with [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") and the [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military") to defeat the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") in a pan-[galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") conflict. However, relations between the High Council and Palpatine became strained during the war, especially after Jedi Knight [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was appointed to the Council's ranks to represent the [Office of the Chancellor](/wiki/Office_of_the_Chancellor "Office of the Chancellor"). The revelation that Palpatine was actually [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious, the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith"), caused several members of the High Council to move against him in a [failed attempt](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") to prevent the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith") from returning to power. Most of the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") were subsequently [purged](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") from [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), allowing Sidious to [declare](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") himself [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY").

## Organization[]

### Composition[]

:   "*How can you be on the council and not be a master?*"  
    "*Take a seat, young Skywalker.*"
:   ―Anakin Skywalker and Mace Windu[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![The Jedi Order was governed by a body of twelve Jedi Masters known as the Jedi High Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Jedi_Council_EP_I.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190110205923) [![The Jedi Order was governed by a body of twelve Jedi Masters known as the Jedi High Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Jedi_Council_EP_I.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190110205923)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/17/Jedi_Council_EP_I.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190110205923) 

The Jedi Order was governed by a body of twelve Jedi Masters known as the Jedi High Council.

 

The [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") High [Council](/wiki/Jedi_Council "Jedi Council") was the governing body of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order"). Its composition consisted of twelve [Jedi Masters](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") who were tasked with the responsibility of guiding the Order.[[9]](#cite_note-KothDB-9) They convened as a council to discuss matters of importance to the Jedi[[10]](#cite_note-GalliaDB-10) and make important decisions on the overall Order's behalf.[[11]](#cite_note-Insider_199-11) Of the twelve, five members had life-long positions[[3]](#cite_note-JMM1-3) as permanent members of the Council. Beyond them, four Jedi were given long-term seats in the body, while the final three were given short-term positions.[[12]](#cite_note-SuperGraphic-12) The Council's activities included deliberating [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") events and discerning the will of [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force").[[13]](#cite_note-JediTempleDB-13) If a Jedi elected to take a sabbatical from their Council duties, the member could select a Jedi to temporarily hold their seat on the Council.[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) The High Council also has a historical precedent in not having factions and the times in history they did, it was not considered effective.[[15]](#cite_note-TLF-15) The path to becoming a member of the Council varied.[[11]](#cite_note-Insider_199-11)

The Council's ranks included two notable positions—the [Grand Master](/wiki/Grand_Master "Grand Master")[[16]](#cite_note-YodaDB-16) and the [Master of the Order](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order"). The Grand Master was an honorific bestowed on the oldest and wisest living Jedi,[[17]](#cite_note-UFC-17) and the holder of the title served as leader of the Jedi Order.[[18]](#cite_note-VisDic-18) However, the title could be shared amongst several Jedi, as it had been during the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era").[[19]](#cite_note-Jedi_Council_Revealed-19) The Master of the Order was [elected](/wiki/Democracy "Democracy") by the High Council to serve as their presiding [officer](/wiki/Officer "Officer").[[18]](#cite_note-VisDic-18) During the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"),[[6]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-6) [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") held the title of Grand Master.[[2]](#cite_note-AEYTK-2) Further, he served as Master of the Order in tandem with [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), who also served as Master of the Order at that time.[[11]](#cite_note-Insider_199-11) Both of these titles were held by Yoda during the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars")[[2]](#cite_note-AEYTK-2) after the two titles were consolidated in the lead up to war.[[20]](#cite_note-Rise_of_the_Separatists-20)

### Roles and privileges[]

:   "*Since we are not members of the Council, we cannot involve ourselves in local political skirmishes, unless requested by the Jedi High Council or Senate.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Dooku[[21]](#cite_note-Choices-21)

 [![The High Council enforced the Jedi Code, a set of rules and disciplines that applied to the members of the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Young_Anakin_before_the_Council.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151002173801) [![The High Council enforced the Jedi Code, a set of rules and disciplines that applied to the members of the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Young_Anakin_before_the_Council.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151002173801)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/91/Young_Anakin_before_the_Council.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151002173801) 

The High Council enforced the Jedi Code, a set of rules and disciplines that applied to the members of the Jedi Order.

 

As the governing members, Jedi who served on the High Council held authority to involve themselves in local [political](/wiki/Politics "Politics") matters, whereas the rest of the Order could only officially engaged under the permission from either the Council or the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate").[[21]](#cite_note-Choices-21) Based on expertise, Council members also acted in specific governing capacities for the Jedi Order.[[15]](#cite_note-TLF-15) [Elected leaders of the Council](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order") often served as a key figure whom met with others to discuss dilemmas but important decisions were made in tandem with all twelve members.[[11]](#cite_note-Insider_199-11) They also acted as an arbiter over matters regarding to special circumstances involving the potential inclusion of Jedi candidates, some which included [Verosha Aniseya](/wiki/Verosha_Aniseya "Verosha Aniseya")[[22]](#cite_note-Lost_/_Found-22) and [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker").[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23)

The High Council had an insignia of its own separate from the overall Jedi symbol, with that High Council emblem used on at least one [starship](/wiki/Starship "Starship"), a [Jedi High Council cruiser](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council_cruiser "Jedi High Council cruiser"), to represent the vessel as carrying Jedi leadership.[[24]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-24) Council members often held the Jedi Code in the highest regard and required all Jedi to adhere to its principles. Members such as Yoda[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23) and [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") were notable for staunchly adhering to the Order's ancient traditions.[[25]](#cite_note-WinduDB-25) While the Council tolerated unconventional Jedi, certain tenets were enforced without question; when Qui-Gon Jinn attempted to take Anakin Skywalker as his Padawan and later circumvent the code by [promoting](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi"), Yoda reminded him both it was forbidden to take more than one apprentice at a time and the Council held the ultimate authority in deciding when a Padawan undegoes the [Jedi Trials](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials").[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23)

Members of the High Council could also leave its ranks at their discretion,[[26]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-26) as Jedi Master [Yaddle](/wiki/Yaddle "Yaddle") did when she chose to relinquish her seat on the Council.[[27]](#cite_note-SithLord-27) Individual members could be removed from the High Council by their colleagues.[[28]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-28) In the event of a councilmember's [death](/wiki/Death "Death"), their seat could be offered to another Jedi Master of the High Council's choosing.[[21]](#cite_note-Choices-21) Although it was known that some wayward Jedi used [blasters](/wiki/Blaster "Blaster"), their use was never condoned by the Council.[[26]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-26) Kenobi, one of the last members of the Council, held a lifelong view that blasters were unreliable[[29]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-29) and uncivilized[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) compared to the Jedi [lightsaber](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber").[[29]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-29)

### Headquarters[]

:   "*The most famous of the Jedi temples, located on Coruscant, served as the home of the Jedi High Council and the vast library of data known as the Jedi Archives.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[30]](#cite_note-SotJ-30)

 [![The Jedi Council Chamber was located in the High Council Tower of the Jedi Grand Temple on Coruscant.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Jedi_High_Council_Tower_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130122234723) [![The Jedi Council Chamber was located in the High Council Tower of the Jedi Grand Temple on Coruscant.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Jedi_High_Council_Tower_TPM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130122234723)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/60/Jedi_High_Council_Tower_TPM.png/revision/latest?cb=20130122234723) 

The Jedi Council Chamber was located in the High Council Tower of the Jedi Grand Temple on Coruscant.

 

The High Council resided in the [Jedi Grand Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace"), the most renowned [Jedi temple](/wiki/Jedi_temple "Jedi temple") in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").[[30]](#cite_note-SotJ-30) The Grand Temple was served as both a school and a monastery for the Jedi Order on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"),[[13]](#cite_note-JediTempleDB-13) the [capital](/wiki/Capital "Capital") [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"),[[31]](#cite_note-CoruscantDB-31) located in the [Core Worlds](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds").[[26]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-26) Before the Council was headquartered at Coruscant, the council was located at [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan") and [Ossus](/wiki/Ossus "Ossus").[[3]](#cite_note-JMM1-3) The Temple [ziggurat](/wiki/Ziggurat "Ziggurat")[[4]](#cite_note-CL_2016-4) featured a "distinctive crown of five spires"—four [Council Towers](/wiki/Council_Towers "Council Towers") surrounding the main [Temple Spire](/wiki/Palace_spire "Palace spire"). One of the four spires was the [High Council Tower](/wiki/High_Council_Tower "High Council Tower") which housed the [Jedi Council Chamber](/wiki/Jedi_Council_Chamber "Jedi Council Chamber").[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23) In addition, the [Pinnacle Room](/wiki/Pinnacle_Room "Pinnacle Room"), a chamber located at the top of the Temple Spire, served as a chamber of the High Council.[[32]](#cite_note-Voices-32)

## History[]

### Age of the Jedi[]

#### Old Republic-era[]

The Jedi High Council was first formed during a time of prosperity in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy")[[11]](#cite_note-Insider_199-11) and existed during the days[[33]](#cite_note-Sith_SWE-33) of the [Old Republic-era](/wiki/Old_Republic-era "Old Republic-era"). During that time, however,[[34]](#cite_note-Eras-34) a [rogue Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_rogue_Jedi "Unidentified rogue Jedi") rejected the ways of the light side on the belief that only the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force") could unlock one's true potential. The rogue Jedi's beliefs disturbed the Council, which [exiled](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") the individual. However, the rogue Jedi gathered a following and created a rival Force order, the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith"),[[33]](#cite_note-Sith_SWE-33) during the [Hundred-Year Darkness](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness").[[35]](#cite_note-SW_2015_9-35) The Jedi and Sith warred for countless generations[[36]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Jedi-36) until the [final defeat](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith") of the Sith, which a [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") named [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane") helped facilitate and escaped. Bane reformed the Sith under the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"),[[37]](#cite_note-Dark_Side-37) enabling the Sith Order to survive in secret over the next thousand years.[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23)

#### High Republic Era[]

##### Conflict with the Path[]

The [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era") was marked by the expansion of the Jedi Order's reach across the galaxy,[[38]](#cite_note-The_Rise_of_Kylo_Ren_2-38) in particular the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories").[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) In [382 BBY](/wiki/382_BBY "382 BBY"),[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39) the Jedi found themselves in conflict with the [Path of the Open Hand](/wiki/Path_of_the_Open_Hand "Path of the Open Hand") cult, who believed the Force needed to be "freed" from use.[[24]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-24) After the [Battle of Jedha](/wiki/Battle_of_Jedha "Battle of Jedha"), Jedi Master [Creighton Sun](/wiki/Creighton_Sun "Creighton Sun") reported to the Council, the membership of which permitted him and Knight [Aida Forte](/wiki/Aida_Forte "Aida Forte") a chance to [investigate](/wiki/Mission_to_Dalna_(Sun_and_Forte) "Mission to Dalna (Sun and Forte)") the Path homeworld of [Dalna](/wiki/Dalna "Dalna").[[40]](#cite_note-Battle_of_Jedha-40) Afterward, the Council was met by Jedi Master [Rinn](/wiki/Rinn_(Duros) "Rinn (Duros)") and Knight [Azlin Rell](/wiki/Azlin_Rell "Azlin Rell"), who reported the [mysterious demises](/wiki/Mission_to_Dalna_(Macri_and_Zink) "Mission to Dalna (Macri and Zink)") of Master [Zallah Macri](/wiki/Zallah_Macri "Zallah Macri") and her Padawan, [Kevmo Zink](/wiki/Kevmo_Zink "Kevmo Zink"), on Dalna. Deciding that the Force was leading them to Dalna, Council members [Ela Sutan](/wiki/Ela_Sutan "Ela Sutan") and [Gluth Andoi](/wiki/Gluth_Andoi "Gluth Andoi") would lead their own mission to Dalna. The Jedi presence on Dalna from those missions and even yet more resulted in the Path launching the [Battle of Dalna](/wiki/Night_of_Sorrow "Night of Sorrow"), in which they unleashed more of the creatures that had destroyed Macri and Zink: the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai").[[24]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-24)

During the battle, Andoi was caught off guard by a Nameless, leading to his death at the hands of Path blasterfire and one of the creatures. However, [Path Guide](/wiki/Guide_of_the_Closed_Fist "Guide of the Closed Fist") [Marda Ro](/wiki/Marda_Ro "Marda Ro") ended up turning on her order during the battle, wiping out all of the Nameless aside from the [Great Leveler](/wiki/Great_Leveler "Great Leveler")[[24]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-24) in an action that ended up destroying the Path cave systems. At that time, Jedi reinforcements, among them Master Yoda, had arrived Dalna, helping to turn the tide of battle against the Path. The engagement was, in immediate hindsight, seen as a way in which work between the Republic and Jedi benefitted the galaxy,[[41]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-41) but, in the years after, another argument would emerge that the deaths on Dalna only occurred because of close Jedi-Republic partnership.[[42]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-42) After the battle, Yoda and Sun also agreed to cover up the existence of the Nameless so as to prevent knowledge of the anti-Force-wielder beings from getting out, both promising to research more into the beings on their own.[[41]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-41) In secret, Ro had also escaped from the battle with the Leveler and began a new campaign to "free" the Force[[24]](#cite_note-Path_of_Vengeance-24) in a plot that would carry on over the [Ro family](/wiki/Ro_family "Ro family")'s generations.[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14)

##### Conflict with the Nihil[]

:   **Yarael Poof**: "*We must always strive for peace, but also justice. Peace without justice is flawed, hollow at its core. It is the peace provided by tyranny.*"
:   **Ephru Shinn**: "*I do not believe there has been a single instance of the Jedi getting involved in the military affairs of galactic government that has generated anything but endless complexity.*"
:   **Lahru**: "*So we should strive only for simplicity? The galaxy is not a simple place.*"
:   ―The Jedi High Council discuss the Nihil[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14)

During the later of [Supreme Chancellery](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") of [Lina Soh](/wiki/Lina_Soh "Lina Soh"), the Republic commissioned [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon") at her request.[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) During that time, the title of Grand Master was shared between three Jedi:[[19]](#cite_note-Jedi_Council_Revealed-19) Yoda,[[43]](#cite_note-High_Republic_1-43) [Pra-Tre Veter](/wiki/Pra-Tre_Veter "Pra-Tre Veter"),[[44]](#cite_note-BTS_1-44) and [Xo Lahru](/wiki/Xo_Lahru "Xo Lahru").[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) All three Grand Masters served on the High Council,[[43]](#cite_note-High_Republic_1-43)[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) which included Jedi Masters [Jora Malli](/wiki/Jora_Malli "Jora Malli")[[43]](#cite_note-High_Republic_1-43) and [Stellan Gios](/wiki/Stellan_Gios "Stellan Gios"), who took the seat on the Council once held by his master, [Rana Kant](/wiki/Rana_Kant "Rana Kant").[[45]](#cite_note-Rising_Storm-45) In [232 BBY](/wiki/232_BBY "232 BBY"),[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39) Yoda was on a sabbatical from the Council[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) due to feeling the Force call him elsewhere.[[43]](#cite_note-High_Republic_1-43) As such, Yoda stationed himself on the [Padawan Academic Cruiser](/wiki/Padawan_Academic_Cruiser "Padawan Academic Cruiser") *[Star Hopper](/wiki/Star_Hopper "Star Hopper")*, where he helped train Padawans[[46]](#cite_note-HRA_1-46) and younglings. He selected the [Mon Calamari](/wiki/Mon_Calamari "Mon Calamari") Jedi Master [Ephru Shinn](/wiki/Ephru_Shinn "Ephru Shinn") to take his place on the Council for the duration of his sabbatical.[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14)

 [![Eleven masters on the Jedi High Council of 230 BBY after another member, Stellan Gios, gave his life on Starlight Beacon.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/Shadows-of-Starlight-1-Textless-Cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230810030642) [![Eleven masters on the Jedi High Council of 230 BBY after another member, Stellan Gios, gave his life on Starlight Beacon.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/Shadows-of-Starlight-1-Textless-Cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230810030642)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/Shadows-of-Starlight-1-Textless-Cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20230810030642) 

Eleven masters on the Jedi High Council of 230 BBY after another member, Stellan Gios, gave his life on Starlight Beacon.

 

During the [Emergences](/wiki/Emergences "Emergences") in the aftermath of the [Great Hyperspace Disaster](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_Disaster "Great Hyperspace Disaster"), the Council realized that the Jedi may be needed in the Outer Rim more than they normally were. The Republic's exploration into the Outer Rim brought them as well as the Jedi into conflict with a group of [marauders](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") known as the [Nihil](/wiki/Nihil "Nihil"),[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) a group that had been secretly formed by the Ro family.[[47]](#cite_note-Eye_1-47) Grand Master Lahru convened the High Council to discuss the threat that the Nihil posed to the Republic. The Council came to the conclusion that the Jedi would help the Republic in the coming [Battle of Kur](/wiki/Battle_of_Kur "Battle of Kur"), during which Malli was killed.[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) Without Malli to fulfill the position, Grand Masters Veter and Yoda traveled to Starlight Beacon to confirm Jedi Master [Avar Kriss](/wiki/Avar_Kriss "Avar Kriss")' appointment as the [space station](/wiki/Space_station "Space station")'s new [marshal](/wiki/Marshal "Marshal").[[43]](#cite_note-High_Republic_1-43) [Ry Ki-Sakka](/wiki/Ry_Ki-Sakka "Ry Ki-Sakka") took Malli's place on the Council.[[48]](#cite_note-High_Republic_Show_4-48) After discovering the connection between the Nihil and Dalna,[[49]](#cite_note-HRA_5-49) where the Jedi had fought the Nameless and the Path[[41]](#cite_note-Cataclysm-41) over a hundred years prior,[[50]](#cite_note-Precedent-50) Yoda went missing from the Order at large as he investigated the true nature of the threat the Republic and Jedi faced.[[51]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-51)

Despite the end of the Great Disaster crisis, the [Nihil conflict](/wiki/Nihil_conflict "Nihil conflict") would continue to drag out, which resulted in stronger ties between the Republic and Jedi Order. Soh and her aides grew increasingly willing to push themselves into Council meetings, which concerned Jedi Master [Cohmac Vitus](/wiki/Cohmac_Vitus "Cohmac Vitus") while he and various Jedi debated what ties their Order should have with the reigning government.[[42]](#cite_note-Out_of_the_Shadows-42) In [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY "230 BBY"),[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39) Gios took Kriss's place as the Marshal of Starlight Beacon when she went off on an unsanctioned [mission](/wiki/Battle_for_No-Space "Battle for No-Space") to the [Great Hall of the Nihil](/wiki/Great_Hall_of_the_Nihil "Great Hall of the Nihil"). He gave his life during the [destruction of Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon") at the hands of the Nihil to prevent the collapsing station from hitting the city of [Barraza](/wiki/Barraza_City "Barraza City").[[52]](#cite_note-Fallen_Star-52) Meanwhile, Yoda returned to the Jedi with news.[[51]](#cite_note-Midnight_Horizon-51) The [Eye of the Nihil](/wiki/Eye_of_the_Nihil "Eye of the Nihil") [Marchion Ro](/wiki/Marchion_Ro "Marchion Ro"), a descendant of Marda's who ruled over the Nihil,[[14]](#cite_note-LotJ-14) unleashed Nameless against the Jedi during the fall of Starlight,[[52]](#cite_note-Fallen_Star-52) which convinced the Jedi to issue a recall of all Jedi back to Coruscant while they determined how to fight the Nameless.[[53]](#cite_note-Eye_of_the_Storm_2-53)

In [229 BBY](/wiki/229_BBY "229 BBY"),[[54]](#cite_note-Veter_Death-54) Grand Master Veter was [executed](/wiki/Pra-Tre_Veter%27s_execution "Pra-Tre Veter's execution") by the Nihil on a broadcast shown to the galaxy. Ki-Sakka took his place as a Grand Master.[[55]](#cite_note-Eye_of_Darkness-55) The [following year](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY"),[[56]](#cite_note-Temptation_Date-56) Jedi Master [Elzar Mann](/wiki/Elzar_Mann "Elzar Mann") was offered to take Gios' empty seat on the Council. Mann ultimately declined the offer as he believed the role did not suit him and that it was not the right place for him when he considered where he was meant to be with the [living Force](/wiki/Living_Force "Living Force"), instead knowing it was with Kriss, after she had told him that she loved him.[[57]](#cite_note-Temptation_of_the_Force-57)

##### The Brendok affair[]

 [![Vernasta Rwoh, on behalf of the Council, condemns Sol's actions as a rogue Jedi during a Senate Tribunal.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/VernestraSenateTribunal-TheAcolyte.png/revision/latest?cb=20240727205327) [![Vernasta Rwoh, on behalf of the Council, condemns Sol's actions as a rogue Jedi during a Senate Tribunal.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/VernestraSenateTribunal-TheAcolyte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20240727205327)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/VernestraSenateTribunal-TheAcolyte.png/revision/latest?cb=20240727205327) 

Vernasta Rwoh, on behalf of the Council, condemns Sol's actions as a rogue Jedi during a Senate Tribunal.

 

In [148 BBY](/wiki/148_BBY "148 BBY"),[[58]](#cite_note-Timeline-58) the High Council was contacted by Jedi Master [Indara](/wiki/Indara "Indara") to receive advice on taking in [Mae-ho Aniseya](/wiki/Mae-ho_Aniseya "Mae-ho Aniseya") and [Verosha Aniseya](/wiki/Verosha_Aniseya "Verosha Aniseya") as potential Jedi candidates. The High Council initially protested and did not sanction either separating the twins nor their involvement with the [Brendok coven](/wiki/Brendok_coven "Brendok coven"). After the coven was seemingly killed off in a fire created by Mae and presumed her dead, the Council reclined their decision and inducted Verosha into the Jedi Order.[[59]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-59)

Sixteen years later,[[58]](#cite_note-Timeline-58) the High Council would then learn much of the truth of what took place, with the coven killed in part due to the actions of the involved Jedi stationed on Brendok and the cover-up. However, high-ranking official and [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Vernestra Rwoh](/wiki/Vernestra_Rwoh "Vernestra Rwoh") would frame the murders committed by Mae upon Jedi Master [Sol](/wiki/Sol "Sol"), who was denounced as a rogue Jedi who was found dead and believed to commit suicide. This cover-up would protect the Order's reputation from the Galactic Senate's probing for increased oversight. However, unbeknownst to the High Council and Rwoh, Sol's death and the new cover story also inadvertently hid the involvement of the [Sith](/wiki/Sith "Sith").[[60]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte_(episode)-60)

#### Late Republic Era[]

Early into the final decades of the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"), the High Council was mired with several problems, in which included the growing corruption in the Republic, some, such as Jedi Master Dooku, believing the Jedi Order increasingly disconnected from citizens[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39), and issues arising from policing the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories").[[61]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-61) Sometime in [58 BBY](/wiki/58_BBY "58 BBY") following a [attack during a Dragonfire Air Rally](/wiki/Attack_at_the_Dragonfire_Air_Rally "Attack at the Dragonfire Air Rally")[[62]](#cite_note-62), the High Council learned of Council member [Yula Braylon](/wiki/Yula_Braylon "Yula Braylon")'s usage of her position to protect her [son](/wiki/Arath_Tarrex "Arath Tarrex") from gambling debts, a revelation in which surprised the Council. While removed, she was not barred from the Order and Braylon sought to later atone for her crimes.[[61]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-61) That same year[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39), [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") is initially offered a seat on the Jedi Council shortly after being promoted to Jedi Master, a post he accepts with intent to helping change the Jedi Order.[[61]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-61) However, he would at some point in time leave the Council.[[21]](#cite_note-Choices-21)

 [![Mace Windu was offered a seat on the High Council after the death of Master Katri.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/FuneralofKatri-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20221104053453) [![Mace Windu was offered a seat on the High Council after the death of Master Katri.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/FuneralofKatri-Choices.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20221104053453)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/FuneralofKatri-Choices.png/revision/latest?cb=20221104053453) 

Mace Windu was offered a seat on the High Council after the death of Master Katri.

 

Between around [50 BBY](/wiki/50_BBY "50 BBY") and [48 BBY](/wiki/48_BBY "48 BBY"),[[63]](#cite_note-Choices_date-63) Windu joined the ranks of the High Council as a replacement to Jedi Master [Katri](/wiki/Katri "Katri"), who was killed while on an assignment on the planet [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"). The High Council had dispatched Jedi Masters Windu and [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") to retrieve Katri's body. While Windu adhered to the protocols of their role as Jedi, Dooku insisted on investigating Katri's death and discovered that she had been killed by the [bodyguards](/wiki/Bodyguard "Bodyguard") of [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Larik](/wiki/Larik "Larik"), who was fatally shot in the ensuing skirmish between the Raxians and the Jedi. After the [funeral of Katri](/wiki/Funeral_of_Katri "Funeral of Katri"), the High Council invited Windu to take Katri's seat.[[21]](#cite_note-Choices-21)

In [42 BBY](/wiki/42_BBY "42 BBY"), Dooku gave a speech to the Senate against the Council's advisement to convince them of the Jedi's inability to police the Outer Rim. However, when he later learned of [Serenno](/wiki/Serenno "Serenno")'s invasion by the [Abyssin](/wiki/Abyssin "Abyssin") raiders and asked for the Council's support shortly afterward, the Council sided with the Republic ruling on account of Serenno's expressed neutrality and how it undermined Dooku's speech given he opined they cannot police the Outer Rim but turns to support Serenno, his homeworld. Frustrated with the Council, this event later became a catalyst among several others for Dooku leaving the Order.[[61]](#cite_note-Jedi_Lost-61)

Later into the final decades of the Republic the upper tier[[64]](#cite_note-MundiDBBG-64) of the Jedi High Council consisted of legendary Jedi Masters,[[16]](#cite_note-YodaDB-16) such as Yoda,[[65]](#cite_note-MundiDB-65) the oldest and wisest of the Jedi;[[32]](#cite_note-Voices-32) [Ki-Adi-Mundi](/wiki/Ki-Adi-Mundi "Ki-Adi-Mundi"), a [Cerean](/wiki/Cerean "Cerean") [alien](/wiki/Alien "Alien") with a binary [brain](/wiki/Brain "Brain");[[65]](#cite_note-MundiDB-65) and Mace Windu, a staunch traditionalist and champion of the Jedi Order[[25]](#cite_note-WinduDB-25) who served as the [elected leader of the Jedi Council](/wiki/Master_of_the_Order "Master of the Order").[[66]](#cite_note-Insider_1992-66) A senior member of the Council, Windu worked to maintain the Order's ancient traditions[[25]](#cite_note-WinduDB-25) and guarded it's independence against the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), whom he believed was weak, corrupt, and incapable of defending galactic citizens from evil.[[67]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars:_Character_Encyclopedia_-_Join_the_Battle!-67)

By around [40 BBY](/wiki/40_BBY "40 BBY"),[[68]](#cite_note-40_BBY-68) Jedi Master Qui-Gon Jinn was offered a seat on the High Council, an offer that was agreed upon by all of the Council members at the time but Yoda. Jinn's views had long been considered controversial and Jinn took the offer as a sign that perhaps the Council was becoming more open to new ideas. Following Jinn's rogue actions in regards to the [coronation](/wiki/Coronation_of_Queen_Fanry "Coronation of Queen Fanry") of [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Fanry](/wiki/Fanry "Fanry") of [Pijal](/wiki/Pijal "Pijal"), the Council considered withdrawing its offer, but decided that the offer would stand. Jinn, however, felt that the Force was leading him along a different path and chose to reject the offer, something which he suspected had not happened for hundreds of years.[[69]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-69)

 [![Unbeknownst to the High Council, former councilmember Sifo-Dyas ordered the creation of a clone army to defend the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224151650) [![Unbeknownst to the High Council, former councilmember Sifo-Dyas ordered the creation of a clone army to defend the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224151650)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/39/SifoDyas_file.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224151650) 

Unbeknownst to the High Council, former councilmember Sifo-Dyas ordered the creation of a clone army to defend the Galactic Republic.

 

Prior to the [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo") by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") was removed from the High Council following several notable instances in breaching procedures in recruitment of Jedi candidates[[15]](#cite_note-TLF-15) and for advocating the creation of an [army](/wiki/Army "Army") for the Republic's protection, believing that the galaxy was on the brink of war. In spite of his removal from the Jedi Order's ruling body, Sifo-Dyas secretly commissioned the [Ruling Council](/wiki/Ruling_Council_(Kamino) "Ruling Council (Kamino)") of [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino") to [engineer](/wiki/Bioengineering "Bioengineering") an army of [clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") [soldiers](/wiki/Soldier "Soldier"). The [Kaminoans](/wiki/Kaminoan "Kaminoan") accepted the contract under the belief that the Jedi Master acted on behalf of the Republic. However, Sifo-Dyas' plans factored into the agenda of the Sith, who co-opted the [clone trooper](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") project after arranging the death of Sifo-Dyas by the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate").[[28]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-28) In addition, the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious used Dooku's disillusionment with the Jedi Order and the Galactic Republic to sway him to the Sith cause. Dooku used Sifo-Dyas' access code to erase all information about Kamino from the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives") and was instrumental in bringing the Kaminoan clone army under the Sith's influence.[[27]](#cite_note-SithLord-27)

#### The Chosen One[]

:   "*Agree with you, the Council does. Your apprentice, Skywalker will be.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23)

 [![Anakin Skywalker, the Chosen One, was taken to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant to be evaluated by the High Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/High_Council_Chamber.png/revision/latest?cb=20131116223700) [![Anakin Skywalker, the Chosen One, was taken to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant to be evaluated by the High Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/High_Council_Chamber.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131116223700)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/High_Council_Chamber.png/revision/latest?cb=20131116223700) 

Anakin Skywalker, the Chosen One, was taken to the Jedi Temple on Coruscant to be evaluated by the High Council.

 

In 32 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"),[[6]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-6) Jinn reported two revelations to the Council—the return of the Sith, who the Jedi had not encountered for over a millennium; and the discovery of Anakin Skywalker, a prodigy of the Force whom Jinn deemed the [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") of Jedi prophecy.[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23) The Council was skeptical of the maverick Jedi's claims, however.[[16]](#cite_note-YodaDB-16) Nevertheless, they decided to commit their resources to discovering the identity of the dark warrior who attacked Jinn on [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine"). Moreover, they agreed to meet with Skywalker in order to gauge his [abilities](/wiki/Force_power "Force power") in the Force. Though the former [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") proved exceptionally powerful with the Force, Yoda sensed a considerable degree of fear within him, noting that fear was a path to the dark side of the Force.[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23) Windu also felt that Skywalker was too old to commit himself to the ways of the Jedi and the Force without being distracted by his emotional attachments.[[25]](#cite_note-WinduDB-25) As a result, the Council turned down Jinn's request to train Skywalker.[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23)

The Council ultimately reversed their decision after Jinn perished in a [duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") against [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") who attacked him on Tatooine. In addition, Skywalker's heroic actions at the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo") convinced the Council to accept him into their ranks as the Padawan of the newly-promoted [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") Obi-Wan Kenobi, Jinn's former apprentice.[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23) Despite this, Windu[[25]](#cite_note-WinduDB-25) remained wary of Skywalker, as did Yoda who feared that Skywalker's training posed great danger to the future of the Jedi Order.[[23]](#cite_note-Episode_I-23) Jedi Master Yaddle resigned her seat on the High Council following Jinn's death on Naboo. She later [died](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Works "Duel in the Works") at Dooku's own hands after informing him as such, unable to sway him back to the light despite her sympathies. By killing Yaddle, Dooku became Sidious' new [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice")[[27]](#cite_note-SithLord-27) and adopted moniker "Darth Tyranus."[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

### Clone Wars[]

#### Road to war[]

:   "*You must realize there aren't enough Jedi to protect the Republic. We're keepers of the peace, not soldiers.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Sheev Palpatine[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

 [![The High Council advised Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine during the Separatist Crisis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest?cb=20161015185023) [![The High Council advised Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine during the Separatist Crisis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161015185023)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Chancellors_Office.png/revision/latest?cb=20161015185023) 

The High Council advised Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine during the Separatist Crisis.

 

In the aftermath of the Battle of Naboo, the galaxy experienced increasing political turmoil and instability as thousands of [star systems](/wiki/Star_system "Star system") joined a growing [secessionist movement](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") in opposition to the rule of the Galactic Republic. As both sides drew inexorably towards war, the Jedi Council consulted with Supreme Chancellor Sheev Palpatine. Owing allegiance to the Galactic Senate,[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) the Jedi were duty-bound to protect the citizens of the Republic.[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71) However, Windu noted that the Jedi did not possess the adequate manpower to defend the entire Republic in a pan-galactic war. Around the same time, the life of Naboo Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") was threatened by an [assassination plot](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala"), leading the Council to assign Kenobi and Skywalker to her protection detail at the chancellor's request.[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

Kenobi and Skywalker prevented Amidala's [assassination](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") and captured her attacker, [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell"), but the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") was killed by her partner, [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett"), before she could reveal his identity to the Jedi. In light of the second attack on the Naboo senator, the High Council ordered Kenobi to personally investigate the [bounty](/wiki/Bounty "Bounty") hunter who hired Wesell. Skywalker was instructed to escort Amidala back to her [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") as her bodyguard throughout the investigation. As leader of the political opposition to the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"), Amidala was reluctant to leave the galactic capital of Coruscant while the Senate debated the creation of a [Republic Military](/wiki/Republic_Military "Republic Military"). Skywalker requested Chancellor Palpatine's assistance on behalf of the High Council, to which the chancellor obliged by issuing an executive order compelling Amidala to return to Naboo for her safety.[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

#### The clone army[]

:   "*Did the council ever authorize the creation of a clone army?*"  
    "*No. Whoever placed that order did not have the authorization of the Jedi Council.*"
:   ―Obi-Wan Kenobi and Mace Windu[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

 [![The High Council discovered that the late Sifo-Dyas secretly created a clone army without their approval.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Mace_Yoda_holo.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722223200) [![The High Council discovered that the late Sifo-Dyas secretly created a clone army without their approval.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Mace_Yoda_holo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140722223200)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cb/Mace_Yoda_holo.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722223200) 

The High Council discovered that the late Sifo-Dyas secretly created a clone army without their approval.

 

The search for Jango Fett led Kenobi to the [extragalactic](/wiki/Extragalactic "Extragalactic") world of Kamino, where he discovered the clone army that had been [bred](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") over the last [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") by Kaminoan [scientists](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist"). [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") revealed that the late Jedi Master Sifo-Dyas commissioned the Kaminoan government to create the army approximately ten years before Kenobi's [arrival](/wiki/Mission_to_Kamino_(Separatist_Crisis) "Mission to Kamino (Separatist Crisis)") in [Tipoca City](/wiki/Tipoca_City "Tipoca City"). Kenobi also learned that the bounty hunter he sought was the clone army's [genetic](/wiki/DNA "DNA") [template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template"). He communicated his findings to Yoda and Windu, who confirmed that the High Council did not authorize the creation of clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper"). They took Kenobi's discovery as evidence of that the Jedi's connection to the Force was diminished, having been unable to foresee the creation of a clone army. Although Windu considered informing the Senate, Yoda argued that it would only compound their situation further, forcing the High Council to contend with more adversaries in addition to the Dark [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") of the Sith.[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

Fett left Kamino with his cloned son, [Boba Fett](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett"), after Kenobi tried to apprehend him. Kenobi pursued the [Fetts](/wiki/Fetts "Fetts") to [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") and consequently discovered the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"), an army of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") secretly built for the newly formed [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems"). The High Council and the Galactic Senate received Kenobi's report about the [droid](/wiki/Droid "Droid") army's development on the [Geonosian](/wiki/Geonosian "Geonosian") homeworld as well as the Confederacy's plans for war under the leadership of the former Jedi-turned-Separatist [Head of State](/wiki/Head_of_State "Head of State"), the [Count of Serenno](/wiki/Count_of_Serenno "Count of Serenno") Dooku.[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

#### A galaxy at war[]

:   "*The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Yoda[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70)

 [![Under the High Council's leadership, the Grand Army of the Republic achieved its first victory in the Battle of Geonosis.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Yoda_mace_windu_ki-adi-mundi_battle_of_geonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111116045153) [![Under the High Council's leadership, the Grand Army of the Republic achieved its first victory in the Battle of Geonosis.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Yoda_mace_windu_ki-adi-mundi_battle_of_geonosis.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111116045153)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/10/Yoda_mace_windu_ki-adi-mundi_battle_of_geonosis.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111116045153) 

Under the High Council's leadership, the Grand Army of the Republic achieved its first victory in the Battle of Geonosis.

 

After the Senate [empowered](/wiki/Emergency_Powers_Act "Emergency Powers Act") Chancellor Palpatine to take control of the clone army, the High Council formed a plan to decapitate the Separatist movement before it could escalate into a pan-galactic war. Windu would lead a [Jedi assault team](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") to aid Kenobi on Geonosis while Yoda traveled to Kamino to see the clone army for himself.[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70) The newly formed [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") launched a pre-emptive strike against the [Separatist forces](/wiki/Confederacy_military "Confederacy military") on Geonosis, where the clones achieved "air and ground supremacy against formidable odds under the skillful leadership of the Jedi Council."[[4]](#cite_note-CL_2016-4) During the initial battle, Jedi Council member [Coleman Trebor](/wiki/Coleman_Trebor "Coleman Trebor") was killed by Jango Fett when he attempted to confront Dooku. Fett was killed, in turn, by Windu. The Republic ultimately succeeded in driving the Separatists into a full retreat, but the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") only marked the beginning of the Clone Wars[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70) in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY").[[6]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-6)

Following the death of Coleman Trebor, the High Council began to rotate different Jedi into his seat without confirming if the rotation method would be a permanent assignment for the new Council members, or simply something born out of the chaos of the quickly growing Clone Wars. By the time of the [Cadesura disaster](/wiki/Cadesura_disaster "Cadesura disaster"), Kenobi was given Trebor's seat, but he was unsure if the assignment would be temporary. While he was honored, he was unsure if he had the experience for such a position. Nevertheless, after his actions during the [mission to Cato Neimoidia](/wiki/Mission_to_Cato_Neimoidia_(Kenobi_and_Skywalker) "Mission to Cato Neimoidia (Kenobi and Skywalker)"), it was decided his seat would be permanent.[[72]](#cite_note-Brotherhood-72)

 [![Throughout the Clone Wars, the High Council led the Republic's war effort under Chancellor Palpatine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/PalpatineRepublicArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20210702051029) [![Throughout the Clone Wars, the High Council led the Republic's war effort under Chancellor Palpatine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/PalpatineRepublicArmy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210702051029)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/PalpatineRepublicArmy.png/revision/latest?cb=20210702051029) 

Throughout the Clone Wars, the High Council led the Republic's war effort under Chancellor Palpatine.

 

Throughout the conflict, the Council led the war effort in their capacity as [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") of the Republic Military.[[73]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-73) Members of the Council, such as Windu, spent much of their time on Coruscant, directing the Jedi in their new role as military leaders[[25]](#cite_note-WinduDB-25) while simultaneously coordinating strategy with the [Office of the Chancellor](/wiki/Office_of_the_Chancellor "Office of the Chancellor"). At times they also participated more directly by leading clone troopers into battle on various planets across the galaxy, including [Christophsis](/wiki/Battle_of_Christophsis "Battle of Christophsis"),[[73]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-73) [Ryloth](/wiki/Battle_of_Ryloth "Battle of Ryloth"),[[74]](#cite_note-Liberty_on_Ryloth-74) and [again](/wiki/Second_Battle_of_Geonosis "Second Battle of Geonosis") on Geonosis.[[75]](#cite_note-Landing_at_Point_Rain-75) Despite committing to their wartime responsibilities, the Council continued to serve as [emissaries](/wiki/Ambassador "Ambassador") of the Republic;[[73]](#cite_note-TCWfilm-73) from bringing neutral worlds, such as [Toydaria](/wiki/Toydaria "Toydaria") into the Republic's fold,[[76]](#cite_note-Ambush-76) to healing the ancient rift between [Bardotta](/wiki/Bardotta "Bardotta") and the Jedi Order, the Council served as both [diplomats](/wiki/Diplomat "Diplomat") and [generals](/wiki/General "General") in their efforts to protect and preserve the Republic.[[77]](#cite_note-TDII-77)

#### Trial of Ahsoka Tano[]

:   "*You have our most humble apologies, little 'Soka. The Council was wrong to accuse you.*"  
    "*You have shown such great strength and resilience in your struggle to prove your innocence.*"  
    "*This is the true sign of a Jedi Knight.*"  
    "*This was actually your great trial. Now we see that. We understand that the Force works in mysterious ways, and because of this trial you have become a greater Jedi than you would have otherwise.*"  
    "*Back into the Order, you may come.*"
:   ―Plo Koon, Saesee Tiin, Ki-Adi-Mundi, Mace Windu, and Yoda, commending Ahsoka Tano[[7]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-7)

 [![The High Council expelled Ahsoka Tano, who was accused of treason against the Galactic Republic.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029024016) [![The High Council expelled Ahsoka Tano, who was accused of treason against the Galactic Republic.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131029024016)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/81/ChamberOfJudgement-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029024016) 

The High Council expelled Ahsoka Tano, who was accused of treason against the Galactic Republic.

 

At the height of the Clone Wars, the Jedi Temple on Coruscant became the target of a [terrorist attack](/wiki/Bombing_of_the_Jedi_Temple_hangar "Bombing of the Jedi Temple hangar") that resulted in the bombing of the Temple [hangar](/wiki/Hangar "Hangar")—an act which killed several Jedi, as well as civilians and clones. Alarmed by the assault on a sacred site of the Jedi Order, the Council assigned Skywalker and his apprentice, [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano"), to investigate the incident.[[78]](#cite_note-Sabotage-78) However, Tano was soon framed for the death of [Letta Turmond](/wiki/Letta_Turmond "Letta Turmond"),[[79]](#cite_note-The_Jedi_Who_Knew_Too_Much-79) a [terrorist](/wiki/Terrorist "Terrorist") whom she captured during the initial investigation.[[78]](#cite_note-Sabotage-78) After Tano was [apprehended](/wiki/Capture_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Capture of Ahsoka Tano") and brought back to the Temple,[[80]](#cite_note-To_Catch_a_Jedi-80) the Council was requested by the Senate to expel her from the Order, believing that an internal Jedi trial would lack impartiality. In addition to revoking her Jedi status, the Senate insisted on having Tano transferred to military custody so that she could be made to stand [trial](/wiki/Trial_of_Ahsoka_Tano "Trial of Ahsoka Tano") for acts of [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason") against the Republic.[[7]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-7)

 [![After the trial, Tano rejected the High Council's offer to rejoin the Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/AhsokaLeavesTheOrder-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029022852) [![After the trial, Tano rejected the High Council's offer to rejoin the Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/AhsokaLeavesTheOrder-TWJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131029022852)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/cf/AhsokaLeavesTheOrder-TWJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20131029022852) 

After the trial, Tano rejected the High Council's offer to rejoin the Order.

 

Following a debate, the Council concluded that there was sufficient evidence to convict Tano as a traitor to the Republic. Additionally, Windu asserted that protecting Tano could be regarded as an act of opposition to the Senate. Though it was not a unanimous decision, the Council chose to comply with the Senate and expelled Tano from the Order, turning her over to a Republic military tribunal. During the trial, Tano was defended by Senator Padmé Amidala and prosecuted by [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin"), who advocated the death penalty for Tano. Ultimately, Tano was cleared of all charges after Skywalker discovered the real traitor: Tano's friend and fellow Padawan [Barriss Offee](/wiki/Barriss_Offee "Barriss Offee"), a fallen Jedi who believed that the Order was too violent and that the Republic on the verge of becoming a failed state. In light of Tano's innocence, the Council apologized, with [Plo Koon](/wiki/Plo_Koon "Plo Koon") admitting that they were wrong to accuse her of disloyalty. Mundi, Tiin, and Windu observed that she had passed a [great trial](/wiki/Jedi_Trials "Jedi Trials") in her training, making her a greater Jedi in the process. The Council offered to welcome her back into the Jedi Order, but to their surprise and Skywalker's dismay, Tano rejected the offer and instead chose to search for a new path in life, damaged by the Council's collective lack of faith in her.[[7]](#cite_note-The_Wrong_Jedi-7)

#### Sith conspiracy[]

:   "*Cover up this discovery we must. No one, not even the Chancellor, may know.*"
:   ―Yoda, to the Jedi High Council and Anakin Skywalker[[81]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-81)

Though preoccupied with the Clone War, the High Council conducted a secret investigation into Sifo-Dyas' death after [his lightsaber](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas%27s_lightsaber "Sifo-Dyas's lightsaber") was found by Jedi General Plo Koon. The Council was disturbed to discover that the Sith participated in the creation of Sifo-Dyas' clone army. While the Council did not understand why their enemy provided the Jedi with the means to defend the Republic, Windu noted with caution that such a revelation would undermine public confidence in the Jedi, the Republic, and the war effort. Citing the valiant service and loyalty of their clone soldiers, as well as the need to bring a swift and decisive end to the war, Yoda declared that the Council would not inform anyone, even the chancellor, of the Sith's involvement in the origin of the clone army.[[81]](#cite_note-The_Lost_One-81)

#### Voices from beyond[]

:   "*Master Yoda, you are older and wiser than any living Jedi, but this does not mean you are beyond the corruption of the dark side.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Yoda[[32]](#cite_note-Voices-32)

 [![Puzzled by a great mystery, Yoda sought the aid of his fellow Masters on the High Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224044854) [![Puzzled by a great mystery, Yoda sought the aid of his fellow Masters on the High Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224044854)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b8/EpGuide611.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224044854) 

Puzzled by a great mystery, Yoda sought the aid of his fellow Masters on the High Council.

 

As the Council investigated the Sith's role in the clone army's creation, Yoda revealed to his colleagues that the [spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") of Qui-Gon Jinn communicated with him from beyond death. However, everything the Jedi knew about the Force suggested that the ability to retain one's own identity after death was impossible. As such, their reactions ranged from concern to skepticism and suspicion. Kenobi believed that Yoda was simply under duress due to the war, but Mundi opined that the ancient Jedi Master was possibly falling to the influence of the dark side. With the Council unable to reach a consensus on Yoda's mental well-being, Windu ordered the [Jedi Temple Guard](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_Guard "Jedi Temple Guard") to monitor his activities as a precaution. With Skywalker's assistance, Yoda escaped from the Jedi Temple,[[32]](#cite_note-Voices-32) embarking on a quest that ultimately led to his discovery of the ability to preserve his identity after becoming one with the Force.[[82]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-82)

#### Assassinate Dooku[]

:   "*Isn't protecting the innocent the very definition of what it means to be a Jedi? We are failing the Republic and its citizens. We must stop this—*now*.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to the Jedi High Council[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71)

 [![The Mahranee massacre pushed the High Council to adopt a plan to assassinate Count Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Council_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130726094932) [![The Mahranee massacre pushed the High Council to adopt a plan to assassinate Count Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Council_RotS.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130726094932)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Council_RotS.png/revision/latest?cb=20130726094932) 

The Mahranee massacre pushed the High Council to adopt a plan to assassinate Count Dooku.

 

By [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"),[[6]](#cite_note-Galactic_Atlas-6) almost three standard years after the first battle of the Clone Wars, the Republic loyalist world of [Mahranee](/wiki/Mahranee "Mahranee") was [conquered](/wiki/Atrocity_on_Mahranee "Atrocity on Mahranee") by a Separatist invasion force. After claiming the planet and its resources for the Confederacy, Count Dooku ordered the deaths of all [Mahran](/wiki/Mahran "Mahran") [refugees](/wiki/Refugee "Refugee") before they could be evacuated from their fallen homeworld. Dismayed by the recent Mahran genocide, the Jedi Council resolved to the end the conflict once and for all by assassinating Dooku. Though Kenobi initially objected to the method of assassination, Windu stressed that it was the Council's obligation to utilize every option at their disposal for the sake of the Republic and its citizens. Windu's argument, combined with the Jedi's duty to the Republic, convinced the Council to sanction the mission. On Kenobi's recommendation, they assigned the task to the maverick Jedi Master [Quinlan Vos](/wiki/Quinlan_Vos "Quinlan Vos") due to his experience with covert assignments.[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71)

In addition to Vos, the Council determined that Dooku's former apprentice, [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress"), was also critical to the success of the mission. To that end, Kenobi tasked Vos with gaining Ventress' trust in order to ultimately secure her support against Dooku. However, despite earning her respect, Vos' relationship with Ventress became increasingly personal, leading the former to break his Jedi vows and move closer to the dark side of the Force.[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71)

After losing contact with Vos for a time, the Council learned from Ventress that not only had the mission failed, but Vos was also taken as a [prisoner](/wiki/Prisoner "Prisoner") of Dooku. Though she was regarded with suspicion by the Jedi, particularly Windu and Skywalker, who blamed her for the failure of the mission, the Council offered to grant her amnesty in return for her cooperation in the rescue of Vos. Together with Dooku's former acolyte, the Jedi successfully retrieved Vos, although Ventress was convinced that he had fallen to the dark side by becoming the count's new disciple. The Council initially did not share Ventress' suspicions, but nonetheless pardoned her in accordance with their arrangement.[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71)

 [![The High Council's agent, Quinlan Vos, recruited Asajj Ventress for the mission to kill Dooku.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/Dark_Disciple_Cover_Detail.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151124230540) [![The High Council's agent, Quinlan Vos, recruited Asajj Ventress for the mission to kill Dooku.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/Dark_Disciple_Cover_Detail.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20151124230540)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/03/Dark_Disciple_Cover_Detail.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151124230540) 

The High Council's agent, Quinlan Vos, recruited Asajj Ventress for the mission to kill Dooku.

 

Vos's deception did not last long, however. Yoda, who began to suspect that Vos had indeed become a traitor, came to sense the dark side within him. At Windu's suggestion, the Council considered having him executed, but after pleas from Kenobi, they dispatched Vos to make a second attempt on Dooku's life as a test of loyalty. They also reluctantly agreed to allow Ventress to participate in the mission after she revealed that the count was scheduled to travel to the planet [Christophsis](/wiki/Christophsis "Christophsis"). At the same time, Kenobi was instructed to execute Vos if he revealed himself as a traitor to the Jedi and the Republic.[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71)

While Dooku ultimately survived the Jedi's [second assassination attempt](/wiki/Second_battle_of_Christophsis "Second battle of Christophsis"), the Council learned that Vos had embraced the dark side and committed several acts of treason, including the murder of two Jedi—[Akar-Deshu](/wiki/Akar-Deshu "Akar-Deshu") and [Kav Bayons](/wiki/Kav_Bayons "Kav Bayons"). However, Vos renounced the dark side and took responsibility for his actions after Ventress saved his life by sacrificing her own. With some persuasion from Kenobi, who argued that the decision to assassinate Dooku was morally wrong and the cause of Vos' fall, the Council forgave Vos by welcoming him back into the fold of the Jedi Order.[[71]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-71)

#### Fall of the Republic[]

##### The Chancellor's representative[]

:   "*Allow this appointment lightly the council does not. Disturbing is this move by Chancellor Palpatine.*"
:   ―Yoda, to Anakin Skywalker[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

During the [Battle of Coruscant](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant"), Count Dooku was killed by Anakin Skywalker. With the death of the Confederate head of state, the remaining [Separatist leaders](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") fled into hiding while command of the battle droid army passed to General [Grievous](/wiki/Grievous "Grievous"), making him the next high-profile target of both the Republic and the Jedi Order. Palpatine assured Windu that the Senate would vote to continue the war as long as the general remained alive and free, to which the Jedi Council responded by prioritizing the hunt for Grievous. By now, the relationship between the Council and the chancellor had grown increasingly strained; Palpatine's gradual accumulation of wartime powers only raised their suspicions.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) Though they initially accepted the chancellor's empowerment in order to quickly mobilize the clone army for war,[[70]](#cite_note-Episode_II-70) the gradual expansion of his control over the Republic caused the Council to become wary of Palpatine's motives.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![The High Council was disturbed by Chancellor Palpatine's decision to appoint Skywalker to their ranks.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Councilrots.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090915231817) [![The High Council was disturbed by Chancellor Palpatine's decision to appoint Skywalker to their ranks.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Councilrots.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090915231817)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/44/Councilrots.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090915231817) 

The High Council was disturbed by Chancellor Palpatine's decision to appoint Skywalker to their ranks.

 

In addition to the supplementary powers given to the chancellor by the Senate, the Council was even more disturbed by Palpatine's decision to appoint Skywalker as his liaison to the ruling body of the Jedi Order. Skywalker's appointment to the Council's ranks at his age was unprecedented; he would be the youngest Jedi to serve on the Council, and although he was counted among the finest warriors of the Order, he had not yet achieved the rank of Jedi Master. Despite their disdain at this move by Palpatine, the Council grudgingly accepted his decision, but on a condition—Skywalker would have a seat on the Council, but not the rank of Master, making him the only Jedi to hold this distinction throughout the history of the Order. In truth, the Council only cooperated with the chancellor so that Skywalker would be in the ideal position to monitor Palpatine's activities. Skywalker, however, felt insulted at not being granted the rank of Master, and was unenthusiastic about his unofficial assignment, regarding espionage against the chancellor as an act of treason. Kenobi disagreed and asserted that the Council's loyalty was to the Senate rather than its leader, who managed to stay in office far beyond what his constitutional term limit would allow.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

##### Conflict with the Chancellor[]

:   "*I sense a plot to destroy the Jedi. The dark side of the Force surrounds the chancellor.*"  
    "*If he does not give up his emergency powers after the destruction of Grievous, then he should be removed from office.*"  
    "*The Jedi Council would have to take control of the senate… in order to secure a peaceful transition.*"  
    "*To a dark place this line of thought will carry us. Great care we must take.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, Ki-Adi-Mundi, and Yoda[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![Chancellor Palpatine's increasing authority motivated the High Council to contemplate his removal from office.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Palp_trustme.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070114040526) [![Chancellor Palpatine's increasing authority motivated the High Council to contemplate his removal from office.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Palp_trustme.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20070114040526)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9a/Palp_trustme.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20070114040526) 

Chancellor Palpatine's increasing authority motivated the High Council to contemplate his removal from office.

 

After [Clone Intelligence](/wiki/Clone_Intelligence "Clone Intelligence") traced Grievous' position to [Utapau](/wiki/Utapau "Utapau"), Skywalker informed the Council that the chancellor wished to place him in command of the [mission](/wiki/Battle_of_Utapau "Battle of Utapau") to kill Grievous. Windu sternly informed him that the Council would decide who among their ranks would confront Grievous, regardless of Palpatine's opinion. Believing that a more experienced Jedi was required to bring the war to a decisive conclusion, the Council dispatched Kenobi and the [212th Attack Battalion](/wiki/212th_Attack_Battalion "212th Attack Battalion"). Yet even as the end of the war drew near, the Council remained skeptical about Palpatine's post-war intentions. Windu could also feel the dark side surrounding the chancellor, which caused him to suspect that a plot to destroy the Jedi Order was close to fruition. Frustrated by the chancellor's accumulation of power and the consequent erosion of the democracy that the Republic stood far, the Council began to regard him as a threat to the Republic. It was at this time that the Council started contemplating the possible necessity of forcibly removing Palpatine from office, an act which would necessitate a Jedi takeover of the Senate in order to maintain political stability during the transition to a new government.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

##### Showdown with the Dark Lord[]

:   "*In the name of the Galactic Senate of the Republic, you're under arrest, Chancellor.*"
:   ―Mace Windu, to Sheev Palpatine[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![The fate of the galaxy was decided in a battle between the High Council and Darth Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) [![The fate of the galaxy was decided in a battle between the High Council and Darth Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20111028234030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b9/DuelonCoruscant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111028234030) 

The fate of the galaxy was decided in a battle between the High Council and Darth Sidious.

 

Having groomed Skywalker as his future apprentice, Palpatine revealed his secret identity as Darth Sidious to the conflicted Jedi Knight who, in turn, reported Sidious to Windu. With his suspicions about the chancellor confirmed, Windu sought to save the Jedi Order from destruction by quickly removing Sidious from power. With the support of fellow Council members [Kit Fisto](/wiki/Kit_Fisto "Kit Fisto"), [Agen Kolar](/wiki/Agen_Kolar "Agen Kolar"), and [Saesee Tiin](/wiki/Saesee_Tiin "Saesee Tiin"), he marched into the [chancellor's office](/wiki/Emperor%27s_office "Emperor's office") and declared his intention to arrest Sidious in the name of the Senate, leading to a fierce lightsaber duel between the Dark Lord and the four members of the Jedi Council. Despite their own skills in [lightsaber combat](/wiki/Lightsaber_combat "Lightsaber combat"), the Jedi Masters Tiin, Kolar, and Fisto were slain by Sidious in quick succession. However, Windu was able to hold his own before ultimately emerging as the victor in the duel. By then, he believed that a trial would be useless as Sidious had gained control of the government, and therefore decided to put an end to his life in order to prevent the return of Sith oppression over the galaxy. Before he could deliver the killing strike, Skywalker, who had just arrived at the [Senate Office Building](/wiki/Imperial_Executive_Building "Imperial Executive Building"), disarmed Windu, leaving him defenseless against the torrent of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") that Sidious unleashed on him.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

##### An order in ruins[]

:   "*At last the Jedi are no more.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Yoda[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

 [![During the execution of Order 66, Darth Vader killed a group of Jedi younglings in the chamber of the High Council.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/ChildrenSlaughter.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208034628) [![During the execution of Order 66, Darth Vader killed a group of Jedi younglings in the chamber of the High Council.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/ChildrenSlaughter.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130208034628)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/8b/ChildrenSlaughter.png/revision/latest?cb=20130208034628) 

During the execution of Order 66, Darth Vader killed a group of Jedi younglings in the chamber of the High Council.

 

With the death of the Jedi Order's champion and the subsequent fall of Anakin Skywalker, who became Darth Vader, Sidious issued [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66")—a secret protocol that compelled the clone troopers to betray and murder their Jedi leaders. Aside from Yoda, [Coleman Kcaj](/wiki/Coleman_Kcaj "Coleman Kcaj"), [Oppo Rancisis](/wiki/Oppo_Rancisis "Oppo Rancisis"), and Kenobi, the remaining members of the Council perished along with the majority of the Order during the initial phase of the purge. During the [siege of the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall") by the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion"), a group of younglings hid in the Jedi Council Chamber where they were discovered and killed by Vader. Yoda and Kenobi returned to the Temple in the aftermath of its fall; after killing a garrison of 501st clones, the two Council members discovered Skywalker's role in the attack and ultimately his new allegiance as a Sith.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

Kenobi [confronted](/wiki/Duel_on_Mustafar "Duel on Mustafar") his former apprentice on [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") while Yoda [challenged](/wiki/Duel_in_the_Galactic_Senate "Duel in the Galactic Senate") Sidious to a duel in the [Galactic Senate Building](/wiki/Imperial_Senate_Building "Imperial Senate Building"). Neither Jedi succeeded in their efforts to destroy the Sith, although Vader sustained severe [burns](/wiki/Fire "Fire") and the loss of his [limbs](/wiki/Limb "Limb"), necessitating [cybernetic](/wiki/Cyborg "Cyborg") surgery and a [suit of armor](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_armor "Darth Vader's armor") to ensure his [survival](/wiki/Life_support "Life support"). The Jedi Masters separated in the ensuing [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") with Yoda [exiling](/wiki/Exile_(punishment) "Exile (punishment)") himself to [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah") and Kenobi becoming a [hermit](/wiki/Hermit "Hermit") on Skywalker's homeworld of Tatooine.[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)

### Legacy[]

:   "*No. I'll have a Jedi with me. Kneel. By the right of the Council, by the will of the Force. Cal Kestis. Rise. Jedi Knight. You are ready.*"
:   ―Cere Junda[[83]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-83)

 [![The former home of the Jedi Order and its High Council was turned into the palace of Emperor Palpatine.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c0/ImperialPalace-2020DarthVader6.png/revision/latest?cb=20210623044208) [![The former home of the Jedi Order and its High Council was turned into the palace of Emperor Palpatine.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c0/ImperialPalace-2020DarthVader6.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210623044208)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/c0/ImperialPalace-2020DarthVader6.png/revision/latest?cb=20210623044208) 

The former home of the Jedi Order and its High Council was turned into the palace of Emperor Palpatine.
