Having purged the Jedi Order and its leadership, Sidious [proclaimed](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the birth of a [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order"), the [First Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") that he would rule under the title of [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor").[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8) The Jedi Temple was renamed as the Imperial Palace, becoming the personal residence of [Emperor](/wiki/Emperor "Emperor") Palpatine,[[13]](#cite_note-JediTempleDB-13) and the Jedi Council Chamber was repurposed to serve as his private office.[[84]](#cite_note-Tarkin-84)

The influence of the High Council's legacy echoed through the [knighting ceremony](/wiki/Knighting_Ceremony "Knighting Ceremony"); [Cere Junda](/wiki/Cere_Junda "Cere Junda") recited a ceremonial quote while knighting Padawan [Cal Kestis](/wiki/Cal_Kestis "Cal Kestis"), recalling the High Council's right to bestow the rank of Jedi Knight to apprentices who passed their trials.[[83]](#cite_note-Fallen_Order-83) An apparition of [the Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"), who was once a [Jedi Temple Guard](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_Guard "Jedi Temple Guard"), conferred the status of Jedi Knight on former Padawan [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") in the name of the High Council.[[85]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-85)

In [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"), the same year as the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"),[[86]](#cite_note-Atlas_Updated-86) [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker")—[the son](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") of Anakin Skywalker—began his training in the Jedi arts under Obi-Wan Kenobi. Although Kenobi was killed by Darth Vader during the [rescue](/wiki/Rescue_of_Princess_Leia "Rescue of Princess Leia") of [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"),[[29]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-29) Skywalker remained determined to follow in his [father's](/wiki/Parent "Parent") example and become a Jedi Knight. Guided by the spirit of his first Jedi Master to the world of Dagobah, Skywalker sought out Grand Master Yoda who agreed to complete his training, despite harboring concerns about the similarities between Luke and Anakin. With Yoda's help, Skywalker honed his nascent powers in the Force[[87]](#cite_note-Episode_V-87) and was deemed to be fully trained by the Grand Master on his deathbed. However, before Skywalker could be considered a true Jedi, Yoda declared that he had to defeat his father, Darth Vader.[[88]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-88)

 [![His destiny fulfilled, Anakin Skywalker joined his fellow council members in death as a spirit in the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) [![His destiny fulfilled, Anakin Skywalker joined his fellow council members in death as a spirit in the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201008104501)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/55/JediGhosts-ROTJ.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008104501) 

His destiny fulfilled, Anakin Skywalker joined his fellow council members in death as a spirit in the Force.

 

Their final battle ended with Skywalker's victory over Vader. Resisting the dark side, Skywalker spared his father's life and refused to take his place as Sidious' apprentice. When the Emperor proceeded to [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture") Skywalker for his rejecting the Sith, Vader moved to save his son in an act of self-sacrifice that ended with the destruction of both master and apprentice,[[88]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-88) ending the Sith lineage that began with [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane")[[89]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-89) and fulfilling the prophecy of the Chosen One.[[90]](#cite_note-TSWB-90) In the aftermath of the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"), Luke Skywalker saw the spirits of his late father, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and Yoda[[88]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-88)—all members of the Jedi High Council[[8]](#cite_note-Episode_III-8)—standing beside each other as the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") celebrated its victory on [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor").[[88]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-88)

## Behind the scenes[]

:   "*I've always felt that one of Anakin's downfalls, like it's never that Anakin was innately going to be evil, but the people around him, the Jedi, in their lack of compassion, in being so selfless that they almost forgot to care.*"
:   ―Dave Filoni[[139]](#cite_note-Rebels_Recon_#3.02-139)

According to [Dave Filoni](/wiki/Dave_Filoni "Dave Filoni"), supervising director of both *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* and *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")* animated television series, one of the reasons for Anakin Skywalker's turn to the dark side was the lack of compassion and care of the Jedi. [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger"), the central character of *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars") Rebels*, however, had a very strong family support system by the [people around him](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres") even though he could be tempted by the dark side.[[139]](#cite_note-Rebels_Recon_#3.02-139) The novel *[The Living Force](/wiki/The_Living_Force "The Living Force")* was written to touch on how out of touch the Council was with the wider galaxy during the later years of the Republic, featuring Qui-Gon Jinn effectively demanding they "touch grass" by interacting with people off of Coruscant.[[140]](#cite_note-Touch_grass-140)

[↑](#cite_ref-Temptation_Date_56-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates [Starlight Beacon's destruction](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon") to [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY "230 BBY"). The implementation of the [Guardian Protocols](/wiki/Guardian_Protocols "Guardian Protocols"), which *[Star Wars: The High Republic Character Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_High_Republic_Character_Encyclopedia "Star Wars: The High Republic Character Encyclopedia")* places in [229 BBY](/wiki/229_BBY "229 BBY"), took place one [week](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") after [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon")'s fall according to [*The High Republic – Shadows of Starlight* 1](/wiki/The_High_Republic_%E2%80%93_Shadows_of_Starlight_1 "The High Republic – Shadows of Starlight 1"). As *[The High Republic: Temptation of the Force](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Temptation_of_the_Force "The High Republic: Temptation of the Force")* takes place one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") and six weeks after the destruction of Starlight Beacon and its events span a few [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month"), it must be set in [228 BBY](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY"). 57. [↑](#cite_ref-Temptation_of_the_Force_57-0) *[The High Republic: Temptation of the Force](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Temptation_of_the_Force "The High Republic: Temptation of the Force")* 58. ↑ [58.0](#cite_ref-Timeline_58-0) [58.1](#cite_ref-Timeline_58-1) [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ["Lost/Found" Episode Guide | The Acolyte](https://www.starwars.com/series/the-acolyte/lost-found-episode-guide) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240613105150/https://www.starwars.com/series/the-acolyte/lost-found-episode-guide)) states that the events of *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* take place 100 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Therefore, *The Acolyte* takes place in [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY").     Furthermore, the events of "[Destiny](/wiki/Destiny_(The_Acolyte) "Destiny (The Acolyte)")" and "[Choice](/wiki/Choice "Choice")" take place sixteen [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the present day events of *The Acolyte*, thereby dating the flashback events of *The Acolyte* to [148 BBY](/wiki/148_BBY "148 BBY"). 59. [↑](#cite_ref-Episode_VII_59-0) [The Acolyte logo Celebration](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte") *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* — "[Choice](/wiki/Choice "Choice")" 60. [↑](#cite_ref-The_Acolyte_(episode)_60-0) [The Acolyte logo Celebration](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte") *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* — "[The Acolyte](/wiki/The_Acolyte_(episode) "The Acolyte (episode)")" 61. ↑ [61.0](#cite_ref-Jedi_Lost_61-0) [61.1](#cite_ref-Jedi_Lost_61-1) [61.2](#cite_ref-Jedi_Lost_61-2) [61.3](#cite_ref-Jedi_Lost_61-3) *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* 62. [↑](#cite_ref-62) *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* establishes that the forty-eighth annual [Dragonfire Air Rally](/wiki/Dragonfire_Air_Rally "Dragonfire Air Rally") took place shortly before [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") accepted a seat on the **Jedi High Council**, which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to around [58 BBY](/wiki/58_BBY "58 BBY"). 63. [↑](#cite_ref-Choices_date_63-0) "[Choices](/wiki/Choices "Choices")" depicts [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") gaining a seat on the **Jedi High Council**. [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") established that [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was the youngest to ever serve on the Council. *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the film to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") and Skywalker's birth to [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"). Therefore, Windu must have been at least twenty-two years old. According to the *[Star Wars Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars_Encyclopedia_(series) "Star Wars Encyclopedia (series)")* booklet "[Mace Windu and Other Force Users](/wiki/Mace_Windu_and_Other_Users_of_the_Force "Mace Windu and Other Users of the Force")," Mace Windu was born forty years before the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), which *Star Wars: Timelines* places in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Therefore, Windu gained a seat on the Council no earlier than around [50 BBY](/wiki/50_BBY "50 BBY"). *[Master & Apprentice](/wiki/Master_%26_Apprentice "Master & Apprentice")* further establishes that Windu is part of the Jedi Council at the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of [Nim Pianna](/wiki/Nim_Pianna "Nim Pianna")'s [death](/wiki/Mutiny_on_the_Advent "Mutiny on the Advent"), which *Timelines* dates to [48 BBY](/wiki/48_BBY "48 BBY"). Therefore, the events of "Choices" must take place between these two years. 64. [91.7](#cite_ref-Blade_Date_91-7) [91.8](#cite_ref-Blade_Date_91-8) The present day events of *[Star Wars: The High Republic — The Blade](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_High_Republic_%E2%80%94_The_Blade "Star Wars: The High Republic — The Blade")* take place between the [wedding of Phan-tu Zenn and Xiri A'lbaran](/wiki/Wedding_of_Phan-tu_Zenn_and_Xiri_A%27lbaran "Wedding of Phan-tu Zenn and Xiri A'lbaran") BBY") by *[Star Wars: The High Republic Character Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_High_Republic_Character_Encyclopedia "Star Wars: The High Republic Character Encyclopedia")*. 92. ↑ [↑](#cite_ref-Veter_date_101-0) *[Star Wars: The High Republic: Chronicles of the Jedi](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_High_Republic:_Chronicles_of_the_Jedi "Star Wars: The High Republic: Chronicles of the Jedi")* establishes that [Pra-Tre Veter](/wiki/Pra-Tre_Veter "Pra-Tre Veter") had served on the Jedi High Council for more than two [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") by the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [destruction of Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY "230 BBY"). Therefore, Veter must have joined the Council by [250 BBY](/wiki/250_BBY "250 BBY"). 102. ↑ [102.00](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-0) [102.01](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-1) [102.02](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-2) [102.03](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-3) [102.04](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-4) [102.05](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-5) [102.06](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-6) [102.07](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-7) [102.08](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-8) [102.09](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-9) [102.10](#cite_ref-SWTHR_date_102-10) [SWYT-Logo](https://www.youtube.com/c/StarWars) [Star Wars: The High Republic | Announcement Trailer](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xCat5fXRyyU) on the official *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [YouTube channel](https://www.youtube.com/c/StarWars) ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20200225080419/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=xCat5fXRyyU)) ([Posted on StarWars.com](https://web.archive.org/web/20200227160746/https://www.starwars.com/video/announce-trailer-star-wars-the-high-republic)) states that the events of *[Star Wars: The High Republic](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_High_Republic "Star Wars: The High Republic")* took place 200 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). 103. ↑ [103.0](#cite_ref-Updated_and_Expanded_103-0) [103.1](#cite_ref-Updated_and_Expanded_103-1) *[Star Wars Character Encyclopedia: Updated and Expanded](/wiki/Star_Wars_Character_Encyclopedia:_Updated_and_Expanded "Star Wars Character Encyclopedia: Updated and Expanded")* 104. [↑](#cite_ref-Beware_the_Nameless_date_108-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates [Starlight Beacon's destruction](/wiki/Destruction_of_Starlight_Beacon "Destruction of Starlight Beacon") to [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY "230 BBY"). The implementation of the [Guardian Protocols](/wiki/Guardian_Protocols "Guardian Protocols"), which *[Star Wars: The High Republic Character Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_High_Republic_Character_Encyclopedia "Star Wars: The High Republic Character Encyclopedia")* places in [229 BBY](/wiki/229_BBY "229 BBY"), took place one [week](/wiki/Standard_week "Standard week") after [Starlight Beacon](/wiki/Starlight_Beacon "Starlight Beacon")'s fall according to [*The High Republic – Shadows of Starlight* 1](/wiki/The_High_Republic_%E2%80%93_Shadows_of_Starlight_1 "The High Republic – Shadows of Starlight 1"). As *[The High Republic: Beware the Nameless](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Beware_the_Nameless "The High Republic: Beware the Nameless")*, including the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of Ada-Li Carro, takes place one and a half [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the destruction of Starlight Beacon, it must be set in [228 BBY](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY"). 109. [↑](#cite_ref-Beware_the_Nameless_109-0) *[The High Republic: Beware the Nameless](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Beware_the_Nameless "The High Republic: Beware the Nameless")* 110. ↑ [110.0](#cite_ref-Into_the_Light_date_110-0) [110.1](#cite_ref-Into_the_Light_date_110-1) The events of *[The High Republic: Into the Light](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_Into_the_Light "The High Republic: Into the Light")*, including the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of Adampo on [Inad Komesh](/wiki/Inad_Komesh "Inad Komesh"), take place in [228 BBY](/wiki/228_BBY "228 BBY") per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:IntotheLightDate "Template:IntotheLightDate"). 111. ↑ [111.0](#cite_ref-TFS_Date_Note_111-0) [111.1](#cite_ref-TFS_Date_Note_111-1) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of *[The High Republic: The Fallen Star](/wiki/The_High_Republic:_The_Fallen_Star "The High Republic: The Fallen Star")* to [230 BBY](/wiki/230_BBY "230 BBY"). 112. [↑](#cite_ref-Wayseeker_112-0) *[The Acolyte: Wayseeker](/wiki/The_Acolyte:_Wayseeker "The Acolyte: Wayseeker")* 113. [↑](#cite_ref-Wayseeker_date_113-0) The events of *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* take place in [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY") per the reasoning [here](/wiki/Template:TheAcolyteDate "Template:TheAcolyteDate"). *[Star Wars: The Acolyte: The Visual Guide](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte:_The_Visual_Guide "Star Wars: The Acolyte: The Visual Guide")* establishes that [Indara](/wiki/Indara "Indara") is fifty-four [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") old in *The Acolyte* and also states that she is twenty-six years old during the events of *[The Acolyte: Wayseeker](/wiki/The_Acolyte:_Wayseeker "The Acolyte: Wayseeker")*. Therefore, the events of *Wayseeker* must take place around [160 BBY](/wiki/160_BBY "160 BBY"). 114. ↑ [114.0](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-0) [114.1](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-1) [114.2](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-2) [114.3](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-3) [114.4](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-4) [114.5](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-5) [114.6](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-6) [114.7](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_114-7) *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* 115. [↑](#cite_ref-Dark_Temple_1_115-0) [*Jedi Fallen Order - Dark Temple* 1](/wiki/Jedi_Fallen_Order_-_Dark_Temple_1 "Jedi Fallen Order - Dark Temple 1") 116. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_note_OBW_116-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the event of [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn") became [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku")'s [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") in [68 BBY](/wiki/68_BBY "68 BBY"), when [Jocasta Nu](/wiki/Jocasta_Nu "Jocasta Nu") was the newly appointed [librarian](/wiki/Librarian "Librarian"). 117. [↑](#cite_ref-Dark_Temple_5_117-0) [*Jedi Fallen Order - Dark Temple* 5](/wiki/Jedi_Fallen_Order_-_Dark_Temple_5 "Jedi Fallen Order - Dark Temple 5") 118. [↑](#cite_ref-Sinube_tenure_118-0) In *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")*, [Tera Sinube](/wiki/Tera_Sinube "Tera Sinube") appears on the High Council when [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") is 17 years old. *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the Dooku't birth to [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY"). Therefore, this event occurs around [85 BBY](/wiki/85_BBY "85 BBY"). Sinube was on the council prior to this, meaning he was on the council before around 85 BBY. 119. [↑](#cite_ref-Anakin_Obi-Wan_Adventure_119-0) *[Choose Your Destiny: An Obi-Wan & Anakin Adventure](/wiki/Choose_Your_Destiny:_An_Obi-Wan_%26_Anakin_Adventure "Choose Your Destiny: An Obi-Wan & Anakin Adventure")* 120. [↑](#cite_ref-Date_2_120-0) "[Choices](/wiki/Choices "Choices")" depicts [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") gaining a seat on the **Jedi High Council**. [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") established that [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was the youngest to ever serve on the Council. *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the film to [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") and Skywalker's birth to [41 BBY](/wiki/41_BBY "41 BBY"). Therefore, Windu must have been at least twenty-two years old. According to the *[Star Wars Encyclopedia](/wiki/Star_Wars_Encyclopedia_(series) "Star Wars Encyclopedia (series)")* booklet "[Mace Windu and Other Force Users](/wiki/Mace_Windu_and_Other_Users_of_the_Force "Mace Windu and Other Users of the Force")," Mace Windu was born forty years before the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), which *Star Wars: Timelines* places in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Therefore, Windu gained a seat on the Council no earlier than around [50 BBY](/wiki/50_BBY "50 BBY"). *[Master & Apprentice](/wiki/Master_%26_Apprentice "Master & Apprentice")* further establishes that Windu is part of the Jedi Council at the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of [Nim Pianna](/wiki/Nim_Pianna "Nim Pianna")'s [death](/wiki/Mutiny_on_the_Advent "Mutiny on the Advent"), which *Timelines* dates to [48 BBY](/wiki/48_BBY "48 BBY"). Therefore, the events of "Choices" must take place between these two years. This episode including the [death](/wiki/Death "Death") of [Katri](/wiki/Katri "Katri") on [Raxus Secundus](/wiki/Raxus_Secundus "Raxus Secundus"). 121. ↑ [121.0](#cite_ref-Plo_Koon_Card_121-0) [121.1](#cite_ref-Plo_Koon_Card_121-1) [2015 Topps *Star Wars* Chrome Perspectives](/wiki/2015_Topps_Star_Wars_Chrome_Perspectives "2015 Topps Star Wars Chrome Perspectives") – Jedi Temple Archives Card: [Plo Koon](https://www.tcdb.com/ViewCard.cfm/sid/114595/cid/8022612/2015-Topps-Chrome-Star-Wars-Perspectives-Jedi-vs.-Sith-8-J-Plo-Koon)  ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20230225212431/https://www.tcdb.com/ViewCard.cfm/sid/114595/cid/8022612/2015-Topps-Chrome-Star-Wars-Perspectives-Jedi-vs.-Sith-8-J-Plo-Koon)) 122. ↑ [122.0](#cite_ref-The_Secret_Jedi_122-0) [122.1](#cite_ref-The_Secret_Jedi_122-1) *[The Secret Jedi: The Adventures of Kanan Jarrus: Rebel Leader](/wiki/The_Secret_Jedi:_The_Adventures_of_Kanan_Jarrus:_Rebel_Leader "The Secret Jedi: The Adventures of Kanan Jarrus: Rebel Leader")* 123. [↑](#cite_ref-Dooku_Exit_123-0) *[The Star Wars Book](/wiki/The_Star_Wars_Book "The Star Wars Book")* dates [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku")'s departure from the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") to 42 years before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which is 42 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system") in the calendar system established by *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")*. 124. [↑](#cite_ref-AOTC_124-0) [*Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones") 125. ↑ [125.0](#cite_ref-Sifo_removal_date_125-0) [125.1](#cite_ref-Sifo_removal_date_125-1) [SWInsider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider") "[A Certain Point of View](/wiki/A_Certain_Point_of_View_(department) "A Certain Point of View (department)")" — [*Star Wars Insider* 206](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider_206 "Star Wars Insider 206") states that [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") was removed from the Jedi High Council around thirty-three [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") prior to [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which corresponds to [33 BBY](/wiki/33_BBY "33 BBY") per *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*. Therefore, Sifo-Dyas was removed from the Jedi High Council in around 33 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 126. [↑](#cite_ref-Star_Wars_Character_Encyclopedia:_Updated_and_Expanded_126-0) *[Star Wars Character Encyclopedia: Updated and Expanded](/wiki/Star_Wars_Character_Encyclopedia:_Updated_and_Expanded "Star Wars Character Encyclopedia: Updated and Expanded")* The encyclopedia states that Oppo Rancisis joined Yaddle on the council, and he is shown on the council by 232 BBY, thus making her a member by this point as well. 127. ↑ [127.0](#cite_ref-Citadel_Rescue_127-0) [127.1](#cite_ref-Citadel_Rescue_127-1) [TCW mini logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* — "[Citadel Rescue](/wiki/Citadel_Rescue "Citadel Rescue")" 128. [↑](#cite_ref-Revival_128-0) [TCW mini logo](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars") *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* — "[Revival](/wiki/Revival_(episode) "Revival (episode)")" 129. ↑ [129.0](#cite_ref-DLOTS_19_129-0) [129.1](#cite_ref-DLOTS_19_129-1) [*Darth Vader* (2017) 19](/wiki/Darth_Vader_(2017)_19 "Darth Vader (2017) 19") 130. [↑](#cite_ref-Databank_Billaba_130-0) [StarWars-DatabankII](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") [Depa Billaba](https://www.starwars.com/databank/depa-billaba) in the [Databank](/wiki/Databank_(2014-) "Databank (2014-)") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20210507154505/https://www.starwars.com/databank/depa-billaba)) 131. [↑](#cite_ref-Kanan_7_131-0) [*Kanan* 7](/wiki/Kanan_7 "Kanan 7") 132. ↑ [132.0](#cite_ref-Billaba_return_132-0) [132.1](#cite_ref-Billaba_return_132-1) At the time of getting put into a coma, [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") was not on the Jedi High Council. Upon returning to the Council after coming out of the coma, Kenobi was on the council, and Kenobi was appointed in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). The Council was full after Kenobi took Billaba's spot, however after [Even Piell](/wiki/Even_Piell "Even Piell")'s death in [20 BBY](/wiki/20_BBY "20 BBY"), there was an open spot for her to return to. 133. [↑](#cite_ref-Billaba_19_BBY_133-0) In [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"), which takes place in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"), Billaba is not on the High Council. She was presumably replaced by [Coleman Kcaj](/wiki/Coleman_Kcaj "Coleman Kcaj"). 134. [↑](#cite_ref-TBB_Aftermath_134-0) [TBBtemplate](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch") *[Star Wars: The Bad Batch](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Bad_Batch "Star Wars: The Bad Batch")* — "[Aftermath](/wiki/Aftermath_(episode) "Aftermath (episode)")" 135. [↑](#cite_ref-Brotherhood_date_135-0) *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates the events of [*Brotherhood*](/wiki/Brotherhood_(novel) "Brotherhood (novel)") to [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"). 136. [↑](#cite_ref-Coleman_Kcaj_tenure_136-0) [Coleman Kcaj](/wiki/Coleman_Kcaj "Coleman Kcaj") replaced [Adi Gallia](/wiki/Adi_Gallia "Adi Gallia") on the High Council. He and Rancicis were in *The Clone Wars* episode "[Voices](/wiki/Voices "Voices")" and they and Billaba were on the Council during *[Dark Disciple](/wiki/Dark_Disciple "Dark Disciple")*. Billaba left the Council around 19 BBY to train Caleb Dume in *Kanan* 8, which takes place after *Dark Disciple*, meaning Kcaj could only have served in that year. 137. [↑](#cite_ref-Agen_Kolar_tenure_137-0) Kolar replaced [Eeth Koth](/wiki/Eeth_Koth "Eeth Koth") on the High Council. Koth left the Council in 19 BBY, meaning Kolar could only have served in that year. 138. [↑](#cite_ref-Anakin_tenure_138-0) [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") was made a member of the High Council a very short amount of time before the dissolving of the Council according to [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") which takes place in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY") per *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")*, meaning he only served in 19 [BBY](/wiki/%27ABY-BBY%27_dating_system "'ABY-BBY' dating system"). 139. ↑ [139.0](#cite_ref-Rebels_Recon_#3.02_139-0) [139.1](#cite_ref-Rebels_Recon_#3.02_139-1) [Recon](/wiki/Rebels_Recon "Rebels Recon") [Rebels Recon](/wiki/Rebels_Recon "Rebels Recon") [#3.02: Inside "The Holocrons of Fate" | Star Wars Rebels](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UiXf--t6oZE) on the official *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [YouTube channel](https://www.youtube.com/c/StarWars) ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20181020165454/https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=UiXf--t6oZE)) ([Posted on StarWars.com](https://web.archive.org/web/20190719004133/https://www.starwars.com/video/rebels-recon-inside-the-holocrons-of-fate)) 140.
